[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer-based fuzzing session timed out while exercising the PDF text [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction path. The fuzzer’s main thread remained runnable for over [0m[1;36m28[0m[39m seconds [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minside the Jazzer tracing callbacks and Apache FontBox’s Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m font parsing [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroutines. No crash was reported—only a timeout.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During a fuzzing run of `com.example.PDFExtractTextFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibFuzzer aborted with a “timeout” error after the harness failed to complete [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing within the allotted time. The Java thread dump shows the main fuzzing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthread stuck deep inside Jazzer’s native tracing callback and the Apache FontBox [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mType [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m font lexer/parser logic.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Although no explicit vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., buffer overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is mentioned, this [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcondition corresponds to a hang or performance issue [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpotential denial-of-service [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscenario[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when parsing certain PDF inputs.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The main [0m[1;39m([0m[39m“runnable”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m thread is blocked in  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    `[0m[1;35mcom.code_intelligence.jazzer.runtime.TraceDataFlowNativeCallbacks.traceConstCm[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mpInt[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNative Method[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    and then in  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    `org.apache.fontbox.type1.Type1Lexer.readToken` → `Type1Parser.parseBinary`.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The PDFBox stack frames indicate parsing of a PFB-encoded Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m font:  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    Type1Font.createWithPFB → PDType1Font → PDFontFactory → PDResources.getFont → [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSetFontAndSize.process → PDFStreamEngine.processPage → PDFTextStripper.getText.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFExtractTextFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m simply invokes [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPDFTextStripper on fuzzer-supplied input; it is not the root cause but initiates [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe code‐under‐test.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Apache FontBox’s Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m font handling classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mType1Lexer, Type1Parser, [0m       [2m                [0m
